< review>
I own a vehicle that is notorious for water pump failure. When I started to hear a noise coming from the water pump (no leakage, yet), I purchased a water pump from a dealership with the intention of having West Auto Group do the install. After consulting other owners of this vehicle model, I decided to have other components replaced at the same time, and some fluids changed. Upon the completion of the work, I picked up my vehicle and drove it home, approximately four miles. When I got home, there was coolant coming out on the street. One of the hoses that had been replaced had a hole worn in it from contact with an upper pulley. I called and told them it was leaking coolant. It was the end of the work day and I was told if I needed to bring it back to do so the next day. Well, with the hose compromised, I didn't want to drive it. So the next morning, the mechanic came to my house with a new hose and coolant, changed the hose, and made sure it was the correct length so it would not rub on the pulley. It was a pleasant surprise to find a business that will make good on their service, even if they have to send someone to your house. I will be bringing my vehicle to them for additional recommended services in the future< /review>

We needed our first smog check for our vehicles this year and having not been through the process we weren‚Äôt sure what to expect, especially as it was a star certified test that was needed. First time writing a negative google review, so I'm sure that says something about how significant the experience was.. Extremely unfortunate and disappointing customer service overall. The man in the store was lovely, and let us know that if we were not home to sign for our package of wine (which we knew we would never be on a week day) that we would be able to simply pick it up at a FedEx location (which legally, and understandably, a person over 21 has to be available).. When attempted to set that up, but FedEx informed us that Buffalo Shipping Post had placed a restriction on their package/delivery, and that we would have to reach out to them so that they could request a change in their "restriction". We called Buffalo shipping and spoke to the most unfortunate and rude woman, who raised her voice (never experienced that on this end of customer service), and who stated that we are responsible for an additional $20 fee to "change the address from our home address to the FedEx location"... She refused to make any changes despite their nondescript advertising of their "change of address" policy (no one communicated that to us at check-out when we specifically asked about a FedEx pick-up), and frankly she refused to communicate appropriately ... I would recommend just going with FedEx to begin with, as the cost in the end is about the same, they are easier to deal with, and they were only helpful and accommodating and delivered actual customer service. Again, my first negative review but I have never been spoken to so poorly and I would hate for anyone else to experience that as well considering the numerous other options in Napa for shipping.< /Text>

I think this was the first review I did for Google a couple years back. Well I'm still eating here that should tell you something right there. I like the food very much. You get good sized portions and the food is good. It's always consistent even when I noticed it's the other cook filling in for the main Chef. Guess he needs a day off once in a while. Lol. I recommend the place. Keep up the good work.</review>

<Gmap_id>0x80dd2b365483d899:0x578e7500ae495599</Gmap_id><text>I am always so busy that I never have time to post reviews.  Today, I had to discuss how happy I was with IBI!!!

My son will be starting HS this fall.  As a physician / former high school teacher who appreciates a teacher who installs and insists on excellence, I was very impressed by our first meeting when Mr. Brad Davis spoke to us regarding his expectations from parents and students.  Being impressed by his professionalism and knowledge, it was natural for me to ask him where my son and I should go to have his trumpet inspected, cleaned....  Without hesitation he and 4 parents who overheard our conversation simultaneously stated, "Imperial Band off of Imperial Highway"!  I googled the location and my first thought was, "30 minutes away?????"   Trusting the excited recommendation I drove from my home in Yorba Linda past several music stores wondering why I was recommend to travel this far.
It was obvious the minute I walked in.  I had them evaluate my child's trumpet he had been using for the past 5 years without us ever knowing we had to take it apart, clean it etc....There was a lot that needed to be done and I thought I was going to be charged an exuberant amount of money (they could have since I had no idea what a fair price was).
They gave me a quote and I thought the owner was mis-quoted because it was so low.
I agreed.
My son asked the staff about his new mouthpiece.  His old was was peeling, so a few weeks ago went to a nearby music store and requested a mouth piece for the trumpet. The gentleman reached under the counter and gave us one and states that will be $63.49.

My son was never happy with it.  When he asked for a new one at IBI, the first question was, what size do you need?  We answered, we didn't know there were different sizes.  The IBI staff ( I wish I remembered her name) stated we should never by a mouth piece without trying them in the store.

She pulled out and explained the different sizes and had my son practice scales with each one until he found the one he was most happy with!!!

She taught us how to maintain the instrument daily and periodically.

Than we needed to arrange pick up--we needed it before July 5 which was my sons first sectional session at his high school.

We showed up only a few days before this and the staff stated that because the 4th of July Holiday it will be tough to be done but "let me go talk to the owner".

The owner told us he will have it done on July 4 th at noon.

We showed up on July 4th at noon and it was closed!!

I called the store and Jerry, the owner answered and told us he is in the back of the store finishing up on my sons trumpet and came to open the door.

It was than that I realized that they planned to have the store closed on July 4th but because my son needed it on July 5, Jerry came in on a holiday to finish up the work my sons' trumpet.

I was extremely grateful and embarrassed.  He charged me the very low fee he quoted me and would not let me tip him on my credit card.  He would not accept a cash tip.  He stated, "I am glad it worked out for your boy", let me know if we needed anything else to not hesitate to call and again refused to accept a gratuity even though I was so incredibly thankful for the excellent service, the going above and beyond the call of duty to help my son out with his predicament of needing his trumpet by a certain time.

P.S.  Not sure what "Jacobtoysabx" is reviewing???  I did quote rentals before purchasing a trumpet and the rental prices were lower than 4 other places I went to.<//text>< rate>
